# Web: Trusted Client

## Previous Flag
```
247CTF{da80795f8a5cab2e037d7385807b9a91}
```

## Goal
Developers don't always have time to setup a backend service when prototyping code. Storing credentials on the client side should be fine as long as it's obfuscated right?

## What I learned
```
JSFuck is an esoteric subset of JavaScript, where code is written using only six characters: [, ], (, ), !, and +.
deobfuscate the code:
    https://www.dcode.fr/jsfuck-language
    https://enkhee-osiris.github.io/Decoder-JSFuck/
```

## Solution
```
START CHALLENGE

      </form>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>
```
